
-----title
苏州 (出生地)
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='c1a81aeb271149e69b1e3550a0ba400b_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("c1a81aeb271149e69b1e3550a0ba400b");'><span id='c1a81aeb271149e69b1e3550a0ba400b_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=801&endYear=827')">801-827年</a>，1-27岁</div><div id='c1a81aeb271149e69b1e3550a0ba400b' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=801&endYear=801')">801年</a>　是年庭筠生于吴中，姑系于苏州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=802&endYear=827')">802-827年</a>　是年在吴中。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='bc6b90071963438aa1fed9ebf71bdd47_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("bc6b90071963438aa1fed9ebf71bdd47");'><span id='bc6b90071963438aa1fed9ebf71bdd47_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=841&endYear=841')">841年</a>，41岁</div><div id='bc6b90071963438aa1fed9ebf71bdd47' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>秋庭筠归吴中旧乡。途中作有《和磐石寺逢旧友》<div id='poem_48354' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_48354' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/48354?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和友人盘石寺逢旧友</a><span class='authorDate'>（841年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18032, "唐", "温庭筠", "poem_title_48354")'>温庭筠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_48354_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_48354'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_48354'>楚寺上方宿，满堂皆旧游。<div id='poem_sentence_0_48354_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_48354'>月溪逢远客，烟浪有归舟。<div id='poem_sentence_1_48354_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_48354'>江馆白蘋夜，水关红叶秋。<div id='poem_sentence_2_48354_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_48354'>西风吹暮雨，汀<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作江）</span>草更堪愁。<div id='poem_sentence_3_48354_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_48354'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_48354_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>秋庭筠归吴中旧乡。途中作有《磐石寺留别成公》<div id='poem_48437' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_48437' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/48437?labeling=true' target='_blank'>盘石寺留别成公</a><span class='authorDate'>（841年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18032, "唐", "温庭筠", "poem_title_48437")'>温庭筠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_48437_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_48437'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_48437'>槲叶萧萧带苇风，寺前归客<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作路）</span>别支公。<div id='poem_sentence_0_48437_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_48437'>三秋岸雪花初白，一夜林霜叶尽红。<div id='poem_sentence_1_48437_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_48437'>山叠楚天云压塞，浪遥吴苑水连空。<div id='poem_sentence_2_48437_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_48437'>悠然旅榜频回首，无复松窗半偈同。<div id='poem_sentence_3_48437_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_48437'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_48437_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; -----end

西安

ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=840&endYear=840')">840年4月</a>　在长安。因“等第罢举”，未能参加本年春之礼部进士试。四月作《自有扈至京师已后朱樱之期》，借以抒发未能参试之遗憾。<div id='poem_48324' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_48324' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/48324?labeling=true' target='_blank'>自有扈至京师已后朱樱之期</a><span class='authorDate'>（840年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18032, "唐", "温庭筠", "poem_title_48324")'>温庭筠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_48324_comment'></div><div "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>霞赤</span>数千枝，银笼谁家寄所思。<div id='poem_sentence_0_48324_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_48324'><span class='link' id='poem_sentence_3_48324_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_48324'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_48324_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=840&endYear=840')">840年</a>　是年秋因故未能赴乡荐，原因当是遭人毁谤。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=840&endYear=840')">840年</a>　是年冬作《书怀百韵》，打算自长安赴吴中旧乡远行。<div id='poem_48490' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_48490' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/48490?labeling=true' target='_blank'>病中书怀呈友人</a><span class='authorDate'>（840年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18032, "唐", "温庭筠", "poem_title_48490")'>温庭筠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_48490_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_48490'>开成五年秋，以抱疾郊野，不得与乡计偕至王府，将议遐适。隆冬自伤，因书怀奉寄殿院徐侍御，察院陈李二侍御，回中苏端公，鄠县韦少府，兼呈袁郊、苗绅、李逸三友人一百韵。</div><div id='poem_preface_48490_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(9936, "poem_sentence_0_48490")'>逸足</span>皆先路，穷郊独<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(9203, "poem_sentence_0_48490")'>向隅</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_48490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_48490'>顽童逃<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(3594, "poem_sentence_1_48490")'>广柳</span>，羸马卧平芜。<div id='poem_sentence_1_48490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_48490'>黄卷嗟谁问，朱弦偶自娱。<div id='poem_sentence_2_48490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_48490'>鹿鸣皆缀士，<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(1932, "poem_sentence_3_48490")'>雌伏</span>竟<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_48490", 48490, "Clauses/7/Comments/1")'>非夫</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_48490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_48490'>采<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作菜）</span>地荒遗野，爰田失故都<sup class='reference id='poem_sentence_6_48490'>奕世参周禄，承家学鲁儒。<div id='poem_sentence_6_48490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_48490'>功庸留剑舄，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_48490", 48490, "Clauses/15/Comments/0")'>铭戒</span>在盘盂。<div id='poem_sentence_7_48490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_48490'>经济怀良画，行藏识远图。<div id='poem_sentence_8_48490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_48490'>未能鸣楚玉，空欲握隋珠。<div id='poem_sentence_9_48490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_48490'>定<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(10323, class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_48490'><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(2532, "poem_sentence_11_48490")'>五车</span>堆缥帙，<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(726, "poem_sentence_11_48490")'>三径</span>阖<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(7714, "poem_sentence_11_48490")'>绳枢</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_11_48490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_48490'>适与群英集，将期善价沽。<div id='poem_sentence_12_48490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_48490'><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(3814, "poem_sentence_13_48490")'>叶龙</span>图夭矫，燕鼠笑胡卢。<div id='poem_sentence_13_48490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_48490'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_48490", 48490, "Clauses/28/Comments/0")'>赋分</span>知前定，寒心畏厚诬。<div id='poem_sentence_14_48490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_48490'>蹑尘追庆忌，操剑学<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_48490", 48490, "Clauses/31/Comments/0")'>班输</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_15_48490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_48490'>文囿陪多士，神州试<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(2078, id='poem_sentence_17_48490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_48490'>正使猜奔竞，何尝计有无。<div id='poem_sentence_18_48490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' "poem_sentence_20_48490")'>市义</span>虚焚券，关讥谩<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(3542, "poem_sentence_20_48490")'>弃繻</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_20_48490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_48490'>至言今信矣，微尚亦悲夫。<div id='poem_sentence_21_48490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_48490'><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(196, "poem_sentence_22_48490")'>白雪</span>调歌响，清风乐<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(1656, "poem_sentence_22_48490")'>舞雩</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_22_48490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_48490'><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(9301, "poem_sentence_23_48490")'>胁肩</span>难黾勉<span id='poem_sentence_24_48490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_48490'>兕觥增恐竦<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作悚）</span>，杯水失锱铢。<div id='poem_sentence_25_48490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_48490'>粉垛收丹采，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_26_48490", 48490, id='poem_sentence_27_48490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_48490'>虎拙休言画，龙希莫学屠。<div id='poem_sentence_28_48490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_48490'>转蓬随款段，耘草辟墁<span class='inlineComment2'>（莫千切）</span>垆。<div id='poem_sentence_29_48490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_31_48490'>质文精等贯，琴筑韵相须。<div id='poem_sentence_31_48490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_32_48490'>筑室连中野，诛茅接上腴。<div id='poem_sentence_32_48490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_33_48490'>苇花纶<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作编）</span>虎落，松瘿斗栾栌。<div id='poem_sentence_33_48490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_34_48490'>静语莺相对，闲眠鹤浪俱。<div id='poem_sentence_34_48490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_35_48490'>蕊多劳蝶翅，香酷坠蜂须。<div id='poem_sentence_35_48490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_36_48490'>芳草迷<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(125, "poem_sentence_36_48490")'>三岛</span>，澄波似五湖。<div id='poem_sentence_36_48490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_37_48490'>跃鱼翻藻荇，愁鹭睡葭芦。<div id='poem_sentence_37_48490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_38_48490'>暝<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作冥）</span>渚藏<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_38_48490", 48490, "Clauses/76/Comments/1")'>鸂鶒</span>，幽屏卧鹧鸪。<div id='poem_sentence_38_48490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_39_48490'>苦辛随蓻<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作葝）</span>殖，甘旨仰樵苏。<div id='poem_sentence_39_48490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_40_48490'>笑语空<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(658, "poem_sentence_40_48490")'>怀橘</span>，穷愁亦据梧。<div id='poem_sentence_40_48490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_41_48490'>尚能甘半菽，非敢薄生刍。<div id='poem_sentence_41_48490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_42_48490'>钓石封苍藓，芳蹊艳<span id='poem_sentence_42_48490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_43_48490'>树兰畦缭绕，穿竹路萦纡。<div id='poem_sentence_43_48490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_44_48490'>机杼非桑女，林园异<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(4234, "poem_sentence_44_48490")'>木奴</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_44_48490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_45_48490'>横竿窥赤鲤，持翳望<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_45_48490", 48490, "Clauses/91/Comments/0")'>青鸬</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_45_48490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_46_48490'>泮水思芹味，琅琊得稻租。<div id='poem_sentence_46_48490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_47_48490'>杖轻藜拥肿，衣破芰披敷。<div id='poem_sentence_47_48490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_48_48490'>芳意忧鶗鴂，愁声觉蟪蛄。<div id='poem_sentence_48_48490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_49_48490'>短檐喧语燕，高木堕饥鼯<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作乌）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_49_48490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_50_48490'>事迫离幽墅，贫牵犯畏途。<div id='poem_sentence_50_48490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_51_48490'>爱憎防杜挚，悲叹似杨朱。<div id='poem_sentence_51_48490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_52_48490'>旅食常过卫，羁游欲渡泸。<div id='poem_sentence_52_48490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_53_48490'>塞歌伤督护，边角思单于。<div id='poem_sentence_53_48490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_54_48490'>堡戍标枪槊，关河锁舳舻。<div id='poem_sentence_54_48490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_55_48490'>威容尊大树，刑法避<span class='link' id='poem_sentence_56_48490'>远目穷千里，归心寄九衢。<div id='poem_sentence_56_48490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_57_48490'>寝甘诚系滞，浆<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作酱）</span>馈贵睢盱。<div id='poem_sentence_57_48490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_58_48490'>怀刺名先远，干时道自孤。<div id='poem_sentence_58_48490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_59_48490'>齿牙频激发，簦笈尚崎岖。<div id='poem_sentence_59_48490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_60_48490'>莲府侯门贵，霜台帝命俞。<div id='poem_sentence_60_48490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_61_48490'>骥蹄初蹑景，鹏翅欲<span class='link' id='poem_sentence_62_48490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_63_48490'>百神歆彷佛，孤竹韵含胡。<div id='poem_sentence_63_48490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_64_48490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_65_48490'>触邪承密勿，持法奉吁谟。<div id='poem_sentence_65_48490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_66_48490'>鸣玉锵登降，衡<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作冲）</span>牙向曳娄<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作裾）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_66_48490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_67_48490'>祀亲和氏璧，香近博山炉。<div id='poem_sentence_67_48490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_68_48490'>瑞景森琼树，轻冰莹玉壶。<div id='poem_sentence_70_48490'>内史书千卷<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作帙）</span>，<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(4690, "poem_sentence_70_48490")'>将军画一厨</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_70_48490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_71_48490'>眼明惊气象，心死伏规模。<div id='poem_sentence_71_48490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_72_48490'>岂意观文物，何劳琢珷玞。<div id='poem_sentence_72_48490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_73_48490'>草肥牧騕袅，苔涩淬昆吾。<div id='poem_sentence_78_48490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_79_48490'>昔皆言尔志，今亦畏吾徒。<div id='poem_sentence_79_48490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_80_48490'>有气干牛斗，无人辩辘轳。<div id='poem_sentence_80_48490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_81_48490'>客来斟绿蚁，妻试踏青蚨。<div id='poem_sentence_81_48490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_82_48490'><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(1279, "poem_sentence_82_48490")'>积毁</span>方<span id='poem_sentence_83_48490'>蛇矛犹转战，鱼服自囚拘。<div id='poem_sentence_83_48490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_84_48490'>欲就欺人事，何能逭鬼诛。<div id='poem_sentence_84_48490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_85_48490'>是非迷觉梦，行役议秦吴。<div id='poem_sentence_85_48490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_86_48490'>凛冽风埃惨，萧条草木枯。<div id='poem_sentence_86_48490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_87_48490'>低徊伤志气，蒙犯变肌肤。<div id='poem_sentence_87_48490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_88_48490'>旅雁唯闻叫，饥鹰不待呼。<div id='poem_sentence_88_48490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_89_48490'>梦梭抛促织，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_89_48490", 48490, "Clauses/179/Comments/1")'>心茧</span><span class='inlineComment2'>（一作绪）</span>学蜘蛛。<div id='poem_sentence_89_48490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_90_48490'>宁复机难料，庸非信未孚。<div id='poem_sentence_90_48490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_91_48490", 48490, "Clauses/183/Comments/0")'>听冰</span>狐。<div id='poem_sentence_91_48490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1375721_comment'></div>特蒙俯开严重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1375721_comment'></div>不陋幽遐。<div class='inline' class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1375721_comment'></div>见羊祜之襟情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1375721_comment'></div>既而哲匠司文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1375721_comment'></div>至公当柄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1375721_comment'></div>犹困龙门之浪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1375721_comment'></div>不逢莺谷之春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1375721_comment'></div>今日俯及陶镕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1375721_comment'></div>将裁品物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1375721_comment'></div>辄申丹慊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1375721_comment'></div>更窃清阴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1375721_comment'></div>倘一顾之荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1375721_comment'></div>将回于咳唾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1375721_comment'></div>则陆沈之质。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1375721_comment'></div>庶望于骞翔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1375721_comment'></div>永言进退之涂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1375721_comment'></div>便决荣枯之分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1375721_comment'></div>如翩翻贺燕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1375721_comment'></div>巢幕何依。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1375721_comment'></div>觳觫齐牛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1375721_comment'></div>衅钟将远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1375721_comment'></div>苟难窥于数仞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1375721_comment'></div>则永坠于重泉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1375721_comment'></div>空持拥彗之情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1375721_comment'></div>不识叫阍之路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1375721_comment'></div>不任恳迫之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_74_1375721_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=852&endYear=852')">852年8月</a>　是年八月裴休以兵部侍郎领监铁转运使同中书门下平章事。裴休拜相之后，庭筠有《上裴相公启》<div id='poem_1375714' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1375714' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1375714?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上裴相公启</a><span class='authorDate'>（852年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18032, "唐", "温庭筠", "poem_title_1375714")'>温庭筠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1375714_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1375714'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1375714'>某启。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1375714_comment'></div>闻效珍者先诣隋和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1375714_comment'></div>蠲养者必求仓扁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1375714_comment'></div>苟无悬解。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1375714_comment'></div>难语奇功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1375714_comment'></div>至于有道之年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1375714_comment'></div>犹抱无辜之恨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1375714_comment'></div>斯则没为疠气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1375714_comment'></div>来挠至平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1375714_comment'></div>敷作冤声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1375714_comment'></div>将垂不极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1375714_comment'></div>此亦王公大人之所慷慨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1375714_comment'></div>义夫志士之所歔欷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1375714_comment'></div>某性实颛蒙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1375714_comment'></div>器惟顽固。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1375714_comment'></div>纂修祖业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1375714_comment'></div>远愧孔琳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1375714_comment'></div>承袭门风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1375714_comment'></div>近惭张岱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1375714_comment'></div>自顷爰田锡宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1375714_comment'></div>镂鼎传芳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1375714_comment'></div>占数辽西。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1375714_comment'></div>横经稷下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1375714_comment'></div>因得仰穷师法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1375714_comment'></div>窃弄篇题。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1375714_comment'></div>思欲纽儒门之绝帷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1375714_comment'></div>恢常典之休烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1375714_comment'></div>俄属羁孤牵轸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1375714_comment'></div>藜藿难虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1375714_comment'></div>处默无衾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1375714_comment'></div>徒然夜叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1375714_comment'></div>修龄绝米。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1375714_comment'></div>安事晨炊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1375714_comment'></div>既而羁齿侯门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1375714_comment'></div>旅游淮上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1375714_comment'></div>投书自达。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1375714_comment'></div>怀刺求知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1375714_comment'></div>岂期杜挚相倾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1375714_comment'></div>臧仓见嫉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1375714_comment'></div>守土者以忘情积恶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1375714_comment'></div>当权者以承意中伤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1375714_comment'></div>直视孤危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1375714_comment'></div>横相<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_42_1375714", 1375714, "Clauses/42/Comments/0")'>陵阻</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1375714_comment'></div>绝飞驰之路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1375714_comment'></div>塞饮啄之涂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1375714_comment'></div>射血有冤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1375714_comment'></div>叫天无路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1375714_comment'></div>此乃通人见悯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1375714_comment'></div>多士具闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1375714_comment'></div>徒共兴嗟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1375714_comment'></div>靡能昭雪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1375714_comment'></div>窃见玄宗皇帝初融景命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1375714_comment'></div>遽恻宸襟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1375714_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_53_1375714", 1375714, "Clauses/53/Comments/0")'>收拭</span>瑕疵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1375714_comment'></div>申明枉结。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1375714_comment'></div>刘丞相导扬优诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1375714_comment'></div>苏许公润色昌谟。<div id='poem_sentence_58_1375714_comment'></div>逮及翔泳未安其所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1375714_comment'></div>雨旸不得其和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1375714_comment'></div>匹夫匹妇之吁嗟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1375714_comment'></div>一聚一乡之幽郁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1375714_comment'></div>欲期昭泰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1375714_comment'></div>必仰陶钧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1375714_comment'></div>某进抱疑危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1375714_comment'></div>退无依据。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1375714_comment'></div>偏哭于穷途。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1375714_comment'></div>日月悬空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1375714_comment'></div>独鄣于丰蔀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1375714_comment'></div>伏以相公致尧业裕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1375714_comment'></div>佐禹功高。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1375714_comment'></div>百姓咸被其仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1375714_comment'></div>一物不违于性。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1375714_comment'></div>倘或在途兴叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1375714_comment'></div>解彼右骖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1375714_comment'></div>弹剑有闻。<div id='poem_sentence_83_1375714_comment'></div>与古为徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1375714_comment'></div>此道不诬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1375714_comment'></div>贞明未远。<div id='poem_sentence_88_1375714_comment'></div>缣缃俭陋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1375714_comment'></div>造写繁芜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1375714_comment'></div>干冒尊高。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1375714_comment'></div>无任惶灼。</div><div id='poem_sentence_92_1375714_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=852&endYear=852')">852年6月</a>　是年四月，杜悰自西川节度使调任淮南节度使，约六月，庭筠有《题城南杜邠公林亭》<div id='poem_48293' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_48293' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_title_48293_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_48293'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_48293'>卓氏垆前金线柳，隋家堤畔锦帆风。<div id='poem_sentence_0_48293_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_48293'>贪为两地分<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作行）</span>霖雨，不见池莲照水红。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=852&endYear=852')">852年</a>　是年岁末，有《上封尚书启》<div id='poem_1375722' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1375722' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1375722?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上封尚书启</a><span class='authorDate'>（852年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: id='poem_content_1375722'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1375722'>某迹在泥途。居无绍介。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1375722_comment'></div>常思激励。以发湮沈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1375722_comment'></div>素禀颛愚。夙耽比兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1375722_comment'></div>因得诛茅绝顶。薙草荒田。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1375722_comment'></div>默想劳神。冥搜刻骨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1375722_comment'></div>遂使崇朝览镜。壮齿成衰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1375722_comment'></div>暇日欹冠。元髫变白。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1375722_comment'></div>望将芜菲。来贡文明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1375722_comment'></div>伏遇尚书秉甄藻之权。尽搜罗之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1375722_comment'></div>谁言凡拙。获预恩知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1375722_comment'></div>华省崇严。广庭称奖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1375722_comment'></div>自此乡闾改观。瓦砾生姿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1375722_comment'></div>虽楚国求才。难陪足迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1375722_comment'></div>而邱门托质。不负心期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1375722_comment'></div>一旦推毂贞师。渠门锡社。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1375722_comment'></div>顾惟孤拙。频有依投。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1375722_comment'></div>今者正在穷途。将临献岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1375722_comment'></div>曾无勺水。以化穷鳞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1375722_comment'></div>俯念归荑。犹怜弃席。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1375722_comment'></div>假刘公之一纸。达彼春卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1375722_comment'></div>成季布之千金。沾于下士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1375722_comment'></div>微回咳唾。即变升沈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1375722_comment'></div>羁旅多虞。穷愁少暇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1375722_comment'></div>不获亲承师席。躬拜行台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1375722_comment'></div>轻冒尊颜。伏增惶惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1375722_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1375722_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=852&endYear=852')">852年</a>　是年有《上杜舍人启》<div id='poem_1375728' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1375728' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1375728?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上杜舍人启</a><span class='authorDate'>（852年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18032, "唐", "温庭筠", "poem_title_1375728")'>温庭筠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1375728_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1375728'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1375728'>某闻物乘其势。则彗汜画涂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1375728_comment'></div>才戾于时。则荷戈入棘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1375728_comment'></div>必由贤达之门。乃是坦夷之径。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1375728_comment'></div>是以陆机行止。惟系张华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1375728_comment'></div>孔闿文章。先投谢朓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1375728_comment'></div>遂得名高洛下。价重江南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1375728_comment'></div>惟彼归荑。同于拾芥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1375728_comment'></div>某弱龄有志。中岁多虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1375728_comment'></div>模孝绰之辞。方成笺奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1375728_comment'></div>窃仲任之论。始解言谈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1375728_comment'></div>犹恨日用殊多。天机素少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1375728_comment'></div>揆牛涔于巨浸。持蚁垤于维嵩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1375728_comment'></div>曾是自强。雅非知量。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1375728_comment'></div>李郢秀奉扬仁旨。窃味昌言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1375728_comment'></div>岂知沈约扇中。犹题拙句。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1375728_comment'></div>孙宾车上。欲引凡姿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1375728_comment'></div>进不自期。荣非始望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1375728_comment'></div>今者末涂怊怅。羁宦萧条。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1375728_comment'></div>陋容须托于媒扬。沈痼宜蠲于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_18_1375728", 1375728, "Clauses/37/Comments/0")'>医缓</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1375728_comment'></div>亦尝临铅信史。鼓箧遗文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1375728_comment'></div>颇知甄藻之规。粗达显微之趣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1375728_comment'></div>倘使阁中撰述。试传名臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1375728_comment'></div>楼上妍媸。暂陪诸隶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1375728_comment'></div>微回木铎。便是云梯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1375728_comment'></div>敢露诚情。辄干墙仞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1375728_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1375728_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=852&endYear=852')">852年</a>　是年有《上蒋侍郎启二首》<div id='poem_1375712' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1375712' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1375712?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上蒋侍郎启二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（852年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18032, "唐", "温庭筠", "poem_title_1375712")'>温庭筠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1375712_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1375712'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1375712'>某闻有以疏贱而间至贵者。古人之所讥笑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1375712_comment'></div>有以单外而蕲<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1375712", 1375712, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>末契</span>者。君子之所<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1375712", 1375712, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>兢戒</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1375712_comment'></div>何则。无因以至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1375712_comment'></div>岂庸辨其妍媸。有为而然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1375712_comment'></div>曾不计于能否。有谈嘲异状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1375712_comment'></div>诡激常姿。希彼顾赡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1375712_comment'></div>斯为衒造。则亦受嗤于识者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1375712_comment'></div>见诋于通人者矣。抑又闻三月而行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1375712_comment'></div>士人之常准。十年乃字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1375712_comment'></div>女子之常期。永为干世之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1375712_comment'></div>厥有后时之叹。某寻常爵里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1375712_comment'></div>谬嗣盘盂。离方遁圆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1375712_comment'></div>因陋成寡。亦尝研穷简籀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1375712_comment'></div>耽味声诗。颇识前修之懿图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1375712_comment'></div>盖闻长者之馀论。颛愚自任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1375712_comment'></div>并介相忘。质文异变之方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1375712_comment'></div>骊翰殊风之旨。粗承师法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1375712_comment'></div>敢坠缇缃。伏以侍郎宏继济之机谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1375712_comment'></div>运搜罗之默识。思将菲质。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1375712_comment'></div>来挂平衡。遂扬南纪之清源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1375712_comment'></div>谨效东皋之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_20_1375712", 1375712, "Clauses/40/Comments/0")'>素谒</span>。越石父彼何人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1375712_comment'></div>夙佩遗文。赵台卿敢欺我哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1375712_comment'></div>敬承馀烈。辄以常所为文若干首上献。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1375712_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1375712_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1375713' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1375713' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1375713?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（852年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1375713_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1375713'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1375713'>某闻朔禽违雪。海鸟知风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1375713_comment'></div>苟曰含灵。咸思择地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1375713_comment'></div>况乎谬窥坟素。常禀盘盂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1375713_comment'></div>从师于洙泗之间。擢迹于湘江之表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1375713_comment'></div>能不成周问道。先诣伯阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1375713_comment'></div>故绛侍言。惟从叔向。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1375713_comment'></div>伏惟侍郎禀生成之秀。穷先哲之姿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1375713_comment'></div>言成训谟。信比暄燠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1375713_comment'></div>某率兹孤植。勔彼单家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1375713_comment'></div>持击缶之凡音。嗣操琴之旧事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1375713_comment'></div>于是持挝自警。割席相徵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1375713_comment'></div>味谢氏之膏腴。弄颜生之组绣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1375713_comment'></div>劳神<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_1375713", 1375713, "Clauses/24/Comments/0")'>焦虑</span>。消日忘年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1375713_comment'></div>虽天分不多。尚惭于风雅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1375713_comment'></div>而人功斯极。劣近于讴歌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1375713_comment'></div>顷常撰刺门人。投书齐帅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1375713_comment'></div>蒙垂盼饰。致在褒称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1375713_comment'></div>既而文圃求知。神州就选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1375713_comment'></div>遂得生刍表意。腐帚生姿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1375713_comment'></div>永言栖托之怀。不在翾飞之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1375713_comment'></div>今者商飙已扇。高壤萧衰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1375713_comment'></div>楚贡将来。津涂怅望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1375713_comment'></div>高堂有念。末路增悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1375713_comment'></div>愿持款启之心。先侦生成之施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1375713_comment'></div>倘或洛阳种皓。犹记姓名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1375713_comment'></div>建业张逵。方宏采拾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1375713_comment'></div>则百灵斯毕。一顾为荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1375713_comment'></div>谨以新诗若干首上献。延露蚩声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1375713_comment'></div>皇华下调。有惭狂瞽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1375713_comment'></div>不称仁私。无任依投之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1375713_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1375713_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=852&endYear=852')">852年</a>　是年有《上学士舍人启》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=853&endYear=853')">853年</a>　是年在长安。庭筠应进士试未第，落第后有《上吏部韩郎中启》<div id='poem_1375729' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1375729' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1375729?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上吏部韩郎中启</a><span class='authorDate'>（853年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18032, "唐", "温庭筠", "poem_title_1375729")'>温庭筠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1375729_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1375729'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1375729'>某识异旁通。才无上技。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1375729_comment'></div>幸传丕训。免坠清芬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1375729_comment'></div>衡轭相逢。方悲下路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1375729_comment'></div>弦弧未审。可异前朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1375729_comment'></div>郭翻无建业先畴。稽绍有荥阳旧宅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1375729_comment'></div>故人为累。仅得猪肝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1375729_comment'></div>薄技所存。殆成鸡肋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1375729_comment'></div>分阴屡转。尺涕难收。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1375729_comment'></div>仲宣之为客不休。诸葛之娶妻怕早。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1375729_comment'></div>居惟数亩。不足栖迟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1375729_comment'></div>智效一官。靡能沾沃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1375729_comment'></div>荒凉散社。流寓穷途。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1375729_comment'></div>高堂之瓮社难充。下泽之津蹊可见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1375729_comment'></div>窃以弃茵怀旧。尚动深仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1375729_comment'></div>投钓言情。犹牵末契。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1375729_comment'></div>敢将幽恳。来问平衡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1375729_comment'></div>升平相公简翰为荣。巾箱永秘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1375729_comment'></div>颇垂敦奖。未至陵夷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1375729_comment'></div>倘蒙一话姓名。试令区处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1375729_comment'></div>分铁官之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_19_1375729", 1375729, "Clauses/38/Comments/0")'>琐吏</span>。厕盐酱之常僚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1375729_comment'></div>则亦不犯脂膏。免藏缣素。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1375729_comment'></div>岂惟穷猿得木。涸鲋投泉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1375729_comment'></div>然后幽独有归。永托山涛之分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1375729_comment'></div>赫曦无耻。免干程晓之门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1375729_comment'></div>进退彷徨。不知所喻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1375729_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1375729_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=853&endYear=853')">853年</a>　庭筠作《送李億东归》，姑系于此。<div id='poem_48577' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_48577' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18032, "唐", "温庭筠", "poem_title_48577")'>温庭筠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>六言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_48577_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_48577'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_48577'>黄山远隔秦树，紫禁斜通渭城。<div id='poem_sentence_0_48577_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_48577'>别路青青柳弱，前溪漠漠苔生。<div id='poem_sentence_1_48577_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_48577'>和风澹荡归客，落月殷勤早莺。<div id='poem_sentence_2_48577_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_48577'>灞上金樽未饮，宴歌已有馀声。<div id='poem_sentence_3_48577_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_48577'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_48577_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=853&endYear=853')">853年</a>　是年约作《访知玄上人遇暴经因有赠》，姑系于此。<div id='poem_48329' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_48329' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_content_48329'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_48329'>缥帙无尘满<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_48329", 48329, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>画廊</span>，钟<span ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=854&endYear=854')">854年</a>　是年春，庭筠游河中节度使徐商幕。有《河中陪帅游亭》诗。<div id='poem_48364' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_48364' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/48364?labeling=true' target='_blank'>河中陪帅游亭<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作陪河中节度使游河亭）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（854年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span id='poem_title_48364_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_48364'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_48364'>倚阑愁立独徘徊，欲赋惭非宋玉才。<div id='poem_sentence_0_48364_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_48364'>满座山光摇剑戟，绕城波色动楼台。<div id='poem_sentence_1_48364_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_48364'>添得五湖多少恨，柳花飘荡似寒梅。<div id='poem_sentence_3_48364_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_48364'></div><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_48292_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_48292'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' id='poem_sentence_0_48292'>昔年曾伴玉真游，每到仙宫即是秋。<div id='poem_sentence_0_48292_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_48292'><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(1451, "poem_sentence_1_48292")'>曼倩</span>不归花落尽，满丛烟露月当楼。<div id='poem_sentence_1_48292_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_48292'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_48292_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=855&endYear=855')">855年</a>　是年在长安。春庭筠应礼部进士试未第。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=855&endYear=855')">855年3月</a>　是年三月，吏部博学宏词科考试，庭筠为京兆尹柳熹之子翰假手作赋。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=855&endYear=855')">855年4月</a>　是年四月，约作《为人上裴相公启》，姑系于此。<div id='poem_1375720' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1375720' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1375720?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为人上裴相公启</a><span class='authorDate'>（855年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18032, "唐", "温庭筠", "poem_title_1375720")'>温庭筠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1375720_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1375720'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1375720'>某闻瘦马依风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1375720_comment'></div>悲皆感土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1375720_comment'></div>秋鹰厉吻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1375720_comment'></div>饥即投人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1375720_comment'></div>能知豢养之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1375720_comment'></div>颇识归飞之兆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1375720_comment'></div>是以台卿沥恳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1375720_comment'></div>先告孙宾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1375720_comment'></div>越石栖身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1375720_comment'></div>惟亲晏子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1375720_comment'></div>观贤达始终之趣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1375720_comment'></div>察古今行止之规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1375720_comment'></div>必有良知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1375720_comment'></div>愿谐依托。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1375720_comment'></div>某伶俜弱植。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1375720_comment'></div>憔悴孤根。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1375720_comment'></div>词林无涣水之文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1375720_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_17_1375720", 1375720, "Clauses/17/Comments/0")'>官路</span>乏甘陵之党。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1375720_comment'></div>每持疏拙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1375720_comment'></div>久谢纷华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1375720_comment'></div>既而曳履侯门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1375720_comment'></div>经时不遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1375720_comment'></div>牵裾宪府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1375720_comment'></div>越月而升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1375720_comment'></div>九衢独愧于迷津。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1375720_comment'></div>五省才沾于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_25_1375720", 1375720, "Clauses/25/Comments/0")'>掌庾</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1375720_comment'></div>相公初缔郑栋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1375720_comment'></div>甫润殷林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1375720_comment'></div>宁知蕞陋之姿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1375720_comment'></div>首在陶甄之列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1375720_comment'></div>拔于郎吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1375720_comment'></div>委在弦歌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1375720_comment'></div>元日纵囚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1375720_comment'></div>殊无异政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1375720_comment'></div>清晨探贼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1375720_comment'></div>未报殊恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1375720_comment'></div>岂期遽露精诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1375720_comment'></div>犹烦鼓铸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1375720_comment'></div>近者私门集衅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1375720_comment'></div>同气贻灾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1375720_comment'></div>孀幼流离。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1375720_comment'></div>关河绵邈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1375720_comment'></div>泪变苌宏之血。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1375720_comment'></div>发同园客之丝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1375720_comment'></div>万里销魂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1375720_comment'></div>孤灯吊影。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1375720_comment'></div>盖生人之大痛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1375720_comment'></div>行路之同悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1375720_comment'></div>泉壤长辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1375720_comment'></div>何缘取决。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1375720_comment'></div>人琴并绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1375720_comment'></div>不得申哀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1375720_comment'></div>端居则有愧簪缨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1375720_comment'></div>乞告而曾无事例。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1375720_comment'></div>又以孔怀酷远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1375720_comment'></div>先茔非遥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1375720_comment'></div>永言龟告之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1375720_comment'></div>遂在蝈鸣之月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1375720_comment'></div>倘解其所任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1375720_comment'></div>契彼私心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1375720_comment'></div>绝缅冒于官曹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1375720_comment'></div>获优游于教义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1375720_comment'></div>孤诚所愿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1375720_comment'></div>九死如归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1375720_comment'></div>其或念以艰虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1375720_comment'></div>难于罢免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1375720_comment'></div>亦有虚閒散秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1375720_comment'></div>不漏于幽微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1375720_comment'></div>终鲜之悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1375720_comment'></div>无惭于显晦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1375720_comment'></div>伏增哀迫恳款之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_70_1375720_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a id='poem_sentence_4_48385_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=855&endYear=855')">855年</a>　约是年作《上崔相公启》，亦系代人所撰，其下限在是年崔铉罢相之前，姑系于此。<div id='poem_1375716' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1375716' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1375716?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上崔相公启</a><span class='authorDate'>（855年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18032, "唐", "温庭筠", "poem_title_1375716")'>温庭筠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1375716_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1375716'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1375716'>某闻石苞羁贱。早遇何曾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1375716_comment'></div>魏武尊高。猥知徐晃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1375716_comment'></div>其后咸成閒气。讫立鸿勋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1375716_comment'></div>简册增辉。尊彝动彩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1375716_comment'></div>则道惟熙载。皆资<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1375716", 1375716, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>甄藻</span>之时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1375716_comment'></div>德迈赓歌。必用搜罗之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1375716_comment'></div>是以皇纲克序。茂范咸凝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1375716_comment'></div>某荆氏凡材。雕陵散质。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1375716_comment'></div>谬传清白。实守幽贞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1375716_comment'></div>矍圃弯弓。何能中鹄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1375716_comment'></div>邱门用赋。寻耻雕虫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1375716_comment'></div>常患荒芜。殊非挺拔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1375716_comment'></div>依刘荐祢。素乏梯航。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1375716_comment'></div>慕吕攀嵇。全无等级。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1375716_comment'></div>分甘终老。莫有良期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1375716_comment'></div>既而窃仰洪钧。来窥皎镜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1375716_comment'></div>坟垆下土。敢望颁形。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1375716_comment'></div>瓮盎顽姿。宁希鉴貌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1375716_comment'></div>岂谓不遗孤拙。曲假生成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1375716_comment'></div>拔于泥滓之中。致在烟霄之上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1375716_comment'></div>遂使龙门奋发。不作穷鳞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1375716_comment'></div>莺谷翩翻。终陪逸翰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1375716_comment'></div>此则在三恩重。吹万功深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1375716_comment'></div>空乘变律之机。未得捐躯之兆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1375716_comment'></div>岂可犹希鼓铸。更露情诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1375716_comment'></div>伏念良马嘶风。非堪伏皂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1375716_comment'></div>饥鹰刷羽。终耻栖笼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1375716_comment'></div>诚知豢养之恩。颇有飞翔之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1375716_comment'></div>而又专门有暇。曾习政经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1375716_comment'></div>闭户无营。因窥吏事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1375716_comment'></div>既辨张汤之鼠。深知子产之鱼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1375716_comment'></div>书剑彷徨。年光倏忽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1375716_comment'></div>徒思效用。无以为资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1375716_comment'></div>倘蒙再扇薰风。仍宣厚泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1375716_comment'></div>庶使晏婴精鉴。获脱于在途。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1375716_comment'></div>●8C6B蔑微班。得升于收器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1375716_comment'></div>才闻謦欬。便是扶摇。<div class='inline' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=863&endYear=863')">863年</a>　是年闲居长安。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=864&endYear=864')">864年</a>　是年闲居长安，有《为前邕府段大夫上宰相启》<div id='poem_1375731' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1375731' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1375731?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为前邕府段大夫上宰相启</a><span class='authorDate'>（864年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18032, "唐", "温庭筠", "poem_title_1375731")'>温庭筠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1375731_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1375731'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1375731'>某闻栾氏垂恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1375731_comment'></div>延于十世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1375731_comment'></div>屈生罹谴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1375731_comment'></div>不过三年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1375731_comment'></div>虽行一切之科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1375731_comment'></div>宜听九刑之诉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1375731_comment'></div>某谬因门荫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1375731_comment'></div>获忝朝私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1375731_comment'></div>虽位以恩迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1375731_comment'></div>而官由政举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1375731_comment'></div>累经重事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1375731_comment'></div>皆立微劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1375731_comment'></div>顷年初忝邕南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1375731_comment'></div>颇常弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1375731_comment'></div>事皆条奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1375731_comment'></div>不敢旷官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1375731_comment'></div>冰蘖<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_1375731", 1375731, "Clauses/16/Comments/0")'>自居</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1375731_comment'></div>膏腴不染。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1375731_comment'></div>南蛮俶优。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1375731_comment'></div>边徼先闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1375731_comment'></div>始事详观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1375731_comment'></div>飞章备述。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1375731_comment'></div>黄伯选根基深固。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1375731_comment'></div>溪洞酋豪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1375731_comment'></div>准诏怀来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1375731_comment'></div>署之军职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1375731_comment'></div>李蒙妄因非罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1375731_comment'></div>忽使诛锄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1375731_comment'></div>某离任之初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1375731_comment'></div>滥称遗爱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1375731_comment'></div>伍营校队。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1375731_comment'></div>千里农桑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1375731_comment'></div>叫噪盈途。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1375731_comment'></div>牵留截镫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1375731_comment'></div>爰从初任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1375731_comment'></div>以至罢还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1375731_comment'></div>不戮一夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1375731_comment'></div>闻于众听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1375731_comment'></div>其后既经焚荡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1375731_comment'></div>又遣统临。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1375731_comment'></div>糠籺不充。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1375731_comment'></div>菅蓬自覆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1375731_comment'></div>曾无禄赐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1375731_comment'></div>惟抱忧危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1375731_comment'></div>至无尺绢贯缗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1375731_comment'></div>以为归费。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1375731_comment'></div>及蒙罪状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1375731_comment'></div>焕在丝纶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1375731_comment'></div>以为徒忝官常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1375731_comment'></div>曾无制置。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1375731_comment'></div>且经营甫尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1375731_comment'></div>物力未周。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1375731_comment'></div>拜疏将行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1375731_comment'></div>替人俄至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1375731_comment'></div>仰恩波而不浃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1375731_comment'></div>驻官局以何由。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1375731_comment'></div>懦怯请兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1375731_comment'></div>才非将帅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1375731_comment'></div>今者九州徵发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1375731_comment'></div>万里喧腾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1375731_comment'></div>凭贼请锋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1375731_comment'></div>己至城下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1375731_comment'></div>则以三千土著。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1375731_comment'></div>众寡如何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1375731_comment'></div>两任经年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1375731_comment'></div>曾无掩袭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1375731_comment'></div>虽有烟尘之候。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1375731_comment'></div>不踰朝贡之州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1375731_comment'></div>无劳北军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1375731_comment'></div>己自抽退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1375731_comment'></div>伏念至德建中之际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1375731_comment'></div>长蛇大豕之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1375731_comment'></div>愿报国恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1375731_comment'></div>尽縻家族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1375731_comment'></div>松楸未拱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1375731_comment'></div>带砺犹存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1375731_comment'></div>顾惭无用之躯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1375731_comment'></div>旋漏不私之贷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1375731_comment'></div>侨居乞食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1375731_comment'></div>蓬转萍飘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1375731_comment'></div>生作穷人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1375731_comment'></div>死为丑鬼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1375731_comment'></div>伏惟相公业开伊吕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1375731_comment'></div>朗镜临人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1375731_comment'></div>运值尧汤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1375731_comment'></div>平衡宰物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1375731_comment'></div>伏乞录其勋旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1375731_comment'></div>假以生成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1375731_comment'></div>免令家庙丰碑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1375731_comment'></div>尚垂虫篆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1375731_comment'></div>秋庭陋巷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1375731_comment'></div>长设雀罗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1375731_comment'></div>恋阙伤魂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1375731_comment'></div>临途结欷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1375731_comment'></div>无任恳迫。</div><div id='poem_sentence_94_1375731_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=865&endYear=865')">865年</a>　是年在长安。约六月以后，因宰相徐商之荐，任国子监助教。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=865&endYear=865')">865年</a>　是年在长安。约作《题韦筹博士草堂》，姑系于此。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=866&endYear=866')">866年</a>　是年在长安。任国子监助教，主秋试。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=866&endYear=866')">866年</a>　是年春在长安任国子监助教，有《休浣日西掖谒所知因成长句》<div id='poem_48316' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_48316' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_sentence_1_48316'>日丽<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(5071, "poem_sentence_1_48316")'>九门</span><span class='inlineComment2'>（一作华）</span>青锁<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作琐）</span>闼，雨晴双阙翠微峰。<div id='poem_sentence_1_48316_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_48316'>毫端蕙露滋仙草，琴上薰风入禁松。<div 盱眙

<div class='label1' id='12db331a67614d3aa84ab6f7cc8b478b_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("12db331a67614d3aa84ab6f7cc8b478b");'><span id='12db331a67614d3aa84ab6f7cc8b478b_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=841&endYear=841')">841年</a>，41岁</div><div id='12db331a67614d3aa84ab6f7cc8b478b' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=841&endYear=841')">841年</a>　自邳县南行至盱眙县，有《旅次盱眙县》<div id='poem_48406' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_48406' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/48406?labeling=true' target='_blank'>旅次盱眙县</a><span class='authorDate'>（841年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18032, "唐", "温庭筠", "poem_title_48406")'>温庭筠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_48406_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_48406'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_48406'>离离麦擢芒，楚客意<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作思）</span>偏伤。<div id='poem_sentence_0_48406_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_48406'>波上旅愁起，天边归路长。<div id='poem_sentence_1_48406_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_48406'>孤桡<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作帆）</span>投楚驿<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作岸）</span>，残月在淮樯。<div id='poem_sentence_2_48406_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_48406'>外杜三千里，谁人数雁行。<div id='poem_sentence_3_48406_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_48406'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_48406_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
扬州

onclick='ShowAllusionComment(1052, "poem_allusion_48371")'>为酒求官</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_48371_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_48371'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_48371'>昔年曾识范安成<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作谢宣城）</span>，松竹风姿鹤性情。<div id='poem_sentence_0_48371_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_48371'>西掖曙河横漏响，北山秋月照江声<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_48371_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_48371'>乘舟觅吏经舆县，<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(1052, "poem_sentence_2_48371")'>为酒求官</span>得步兵。<div id='poem_sentence_2_48371_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_48371'>千顷水流通故墅，至今留得谢公名<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_48371_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_48371'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_48371_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_48371'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_48371_0'>⑴ 一作唯向旧山留月色，偶逢秋涧似琴声</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_48371_0'>⑵ 一作玉柄寂寥谭客散，却寻池阁泪纵横</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_48371_comment'></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>秋令，庭筠开始渡江归吴中旧乡。渡江后，有《溪上行》，姑系于此。<span class='inlineComment2'>（姑系于此。）</span><div id='poem_48447' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_48447' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/48447?labeling=true' target='_blank'>溪上行</a><span class='authorDate'>（841年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18032, "唐", "温庭筠", "poem_title_48447")'>温庭筠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_48447_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_48447'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(771, "poem_allusion_48447")'>张翰</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_48447_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_48447'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_48447'>绿塘漾漾烟濛濛，<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(771, "poem_sentence_0_48447")'>张翰</span>此来情不穷。<div id='poem_sentence_0_48447_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_48447'>雪羽䙰褷立倒影，金鳞拨剌跳晴空。<div id='poem_sentence_1_48447_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_48447'>风翻荷叶一向白，雨湿蓼花千穗红。<div id='poem_sentence_2_48447_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_48447'>心羡夕阳波上客，片时归梦<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作去）</span>钓船中。<div id='poem_sentence_3_48447_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_48447'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_48447_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
丹阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='33714e6232304a469cc7c678f7c25898_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("33714e6232304a469cc7c678f7c25898");'><span id='33714e6232304a469cc7c678f7c25898_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=841&endYear=841')">841年</a>，41岁</div><div id='33714e6232304a469cc7c678f7c25898' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=841&endYear=841')">841年</a>　秋庭筠归吴中旧乡。途中作有《开圣寺》<div id='poem_48311' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_48311' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/48311?labeling=true' target='_blank'>开圣寺</a><span class='authorDate'>（841年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18032, "唐", "温庭筠", "poem_title_48311")'>温庭筠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_48311_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_48311'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_48311'>路分溪石夹烟丛，十里萧萧古树风。<div id='poem_sentence_0_48311_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_48311'>出寺马嘶秋色里，向陵鸦乱夕阳中。<div id='poem_sentence_1_48311_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_48311'>竹间泉落山厨静，塔下僧归影殿空。<div id='poem_sentence_2_48311_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_48311'>犹有南朝旧碑在，耻<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作敢）</span>将<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_48311", 48311, "Clauses/7/Comments/2")'>兴废</span>问休公<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作渔翁）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_48311_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_48311'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_48311_comment'></div></div><div class='poemComment' id='poem_comment_48311'><a href='javascript: ShowPoemComment(48311)'>评注</a><span class='inlineComment4'>（点击查看或隐藏评注）</span></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
绍兴
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='30c1f333d41c4743af6db4cca7cb39c0_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("30c1f333d41c4743af6db4cca7cb39c0");'><span id='30c1f333d41c4743af6db4cca7cb39c0_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=842&endYear=842')">842年</a>，42岁</div><div id='30c1f333d41c4743af6db4cca7cb39c0' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>秋在越中。有《题竹谷神神祠》<div id='poem_48456' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_48456' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/48456?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题竹谷神祠<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作谷神庙）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（842年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18032, "唐", "温庭筠", "poem_title_48456")'>温庭筠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_48456_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_48456'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_48456'>苍苍松竹<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作色）</span>晚，一径入荒祠。<div id='poem_sentence_0_48456_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_48456'>古树风吹马，虚廊日照旗。<div id='poem_sentence_1_48456_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_48456'>烟煤朝奠处，风<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作云）</span>雨夜归时。<div id='poem_sentence_2_48456_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_48456'>寂寞东湖<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作湘江）</span>客，空看蒋帝碑。<div id='poem_sentence_3_48456_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_48456'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_48456_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; 萧山

岳阳

ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=856&endYear=856')">856年</a>　是年贬隋县尉，贬前有《上裴舍人启》，旋居襄阳幕。<div id='poem_1375724' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1375724' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_content_1375724'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1375724'>某自东道无依。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1375724_comment'></div>南风不竞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1375724_comment'></div>如挤井谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1375724_comment'></div>若泛沧溟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1375724_comment'></div>莫知投足之方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1375724_comment'></div>不识栖身之所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1375724_comment'></div>孙嵩百口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1375724_comment'></div>系以存亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1375724_comment'></div>王尊一身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1375724_comment'></div>困于贤佞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1375724_comment'></div>伏念济绝气者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1375724_comment'></div>命为神药。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1375724_comment'></div>起僵尸者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1375724_comment'></div>号曰良医。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1375724_comment'></div>自顷常奉绪言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1375724_comment'></div>每行中虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1375724_comment'></div>猥将琐质。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1375724_comment'></div>贮在宏襟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1375724_comment'></div>今则阮路与悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1375724_comment'></div>商歌结恨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1375724_comment'></div>牛衣夜哭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1375724_comment'></div>马柱晨吟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1375724_comment'></div>一笈徘徊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1375724_comment'></div>九门深阻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1375724_comment'></div>敢持幽款。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1375724_comment'></div>上诉隆私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1375724_comment'></div>伏以舍人十六兄法上圣之规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1375724_comment'></div>行古人之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1375724_comment'></div>俯敦中外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1375724_comment'></div>不陋幽沈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1375724_comment'></div>迹在层霄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1375724_comment'></div>足有排虚之计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1375724_comment'></div>身居大艑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1375724_comment'></div>宁无济溺之方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1375724_comment'></div>伏在庭除。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1375724_comment'></div>希闻謦欬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1375724_comment'></div>下情无任。</div><div id='poem_sentence_36_1375724_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
襄阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='e1960b0cf1064a9da6dd5fbf12999e5e_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("e1960b0cf1064a9da6dd5fbf12999e5e");'><span id='e1960b0cf1064a9da6dd5fbf12999e5e_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=856&endYear=856')">856年</a>　至襄阳，为山南东道节度使所辖。徐商予以照顾，留使府署为巡官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=857&endYear=857')">857年</a>　是年在襄阳幕。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=858&endYear=858')">858年</a>　是年在襄阳幕。春，李億登进士第，为状元。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=859&endYear=859')">859年</a>　是年段成式隐于岘山，游襄阳幕，相与唱和，作《答段柯古见嘲》<div id='poem_48282' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_48282' class='poemTitle id='poem_sentence_0_48282_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_48282'>尾薪<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作生）</span>桥下未为痴，暮雨朝云世间少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1375708_comment'></div>□蜗睆伤明。庸敢抚翼<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1375708", 1375708, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>鹓鹏</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1375708_comment'></div>追踪骥騄。每承函素。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1375708_comment'></div>若涉沧溟。亦有丛憏尚存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1375708_comment'></div>笺馀可记。至于缞从墨制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1375708_comment'></div>既御秦兵。绶匪旧仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1375708_comment'></div>仍传汉制。张池造写。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1375708_comment'></div>蔡碣舍舒。荷新滏之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1375708_comment'></div>空沾子野。发冶城之沼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1375708_comment'></div>独避元规。窘类颉羹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1375708_comment'></div>辞同格饭。其为愧怍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1375708_comment'></div>岂可胜言。庭筠状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1375708_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1375708_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1375709' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1375709' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1375709?labeling=true' class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1375709'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1375709'>昨日浴签时光风亭小宴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1375709_comment'></div>三鼓方归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1375709_comment'></div>临出捧缄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1375709_comment'></div>在酲忘答。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1375709_comment'></div>亦以蚳蝝久罄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1375709_comment'></div>川渎皆陨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1375709_comment'></div>岂知元化之杯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1375709_comment'></div>莫能穷竭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1375709_comment'></div>季伦之宝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1375709_comment'></div>益更扶疏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1375709_comment'></div>虽有瀚海叠石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1375709_comment'></div>须阳水号。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1375709_comment'></div>烟城倥咏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1375709_comment'></div>剩出青松。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1375709_comment'></div>恶道遗踪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1375709_comment'></div>空留白石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1375709_comment'></div>扇里止馀乌牸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1375709_comment'></div>屏间正作苍蝇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1375709_comment'></div>岂敢犹弯楚野之弓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1375709_comment'></div>尚索神亭之戟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1375709_comment'></div>谨当焚笔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1375709_comment'></div>不复操觚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1375709_comment'></div>庭筠状。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1375709_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18032, "唐", "温庭筠", "poem_title_48484")'>温庭筠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_48484_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_48484_0'>① 一作和周繇广阳公宴嘲段成式诗。繇诗题，广阳公宴，成式速罢驰骋，坐观花体，或有眼饱之嘲。诗及段荅诗并六韵。</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_48484'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_48484'>齐马驰<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_48484", 48484, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>千驷</span>，卢姬逞十三。<div id='poem_sentence_0_48484_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_48484'>玳筵方喜<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作盻）</span>睐，金勒自䟃𧽼。<div id='poem_sentence_1_48484_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_48484'>堕珥情初洽，鸣鞭战未酣。<div id='poem_sentence_2_48484_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_48484'>神交花冉冉，眉语柳毵毵。<div id='poem_sentence_3_48484_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_48484'>却略青鸾镜，翘翻翠凤篸。<div id='poem_sentence_0_48254_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_48254'>拂巾双雉叫，飘瓦两鸳飞。<div id='poem_sentence_1_48254_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_48254'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_48254_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=859&endYear=859')">859年</a>　是年段成式隐于岘山，游襄阳幕，相与唱和，作《锦鞵赋》<div id='poem_1375701' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1375701' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_content_1375701'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1375701'>阑里花春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1375701_comment'></div>云边月新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1375701_comment'></div>鞻称雅舞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1375701_comment'></div>履号远游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1375701_comment'></div>若乃金莲东昏之潘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1375701_comment'></div>凌波微步瞥陈王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1375701_comment'></div>既蹀躞而容与。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1375701_comment'></div>花尘香迹逢石氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1375701_comment'></div>倏窈窕而呈姿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1375701_comment'></div>擎箱回津。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1375701_comment'></div>惊萧郎之始见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1375701_comment'></div>李文明练。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1375701_comment'></div>恨汉后之未持。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1375701_comment'></div>重为系曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1375701_comment'></div>瑶池仙子董双成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1375701_comment'></div>夜明帘额悬曲琼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1375701_comment'></div>将上云而垂手。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1375701_comment'></div>顾转盼而遗情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1375701_comment'></div>愿绸缪于芳趾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1375701_comment'></div>附周旋于绮楹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1375701_comment'></div>莫悲更衣床前弃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1375701_comment'></div>侧听东晞佩玉声。</div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1375701_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=859&endYear=859')">859年</a>　是年在襄阳幕，有《烧歌》，约作于大中十年至咸通元年居襄阳幕期间之某年春，姑系于此。<div id='poem_48540' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_48540' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/48540?labeling=true' target='_blank'>烧歌</a><span class='authorDate'>（859年）</span><span
