id='poem_sentence_0_48540_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_48540'>微红夕<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作久）</span>如灭，短燄复相连。<div id='poem_sentence_1_48540_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_48540'>差差向岩石，冉冉凌青壁。<div id='poem_sentence_2_48540_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_48540'>低随回风尽，远照檐茅<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作茅檐）</span>赤。<div id='poem_sentence_3_48540_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_48540'>邻翁能楚言，倚插欲潸然。<div id='poem_sentence_4_48540_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_48540'>自言楚越俗，烧畬为<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作作）</span>早<span id='poem_sentence_6_48540_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_48540'>废栈豕归栏，广场鸡啄粟。<div id='poem_sentence_7_48540_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_48540'>新年春雨晴，处处赛神声。<div id='poem_sentence_8_48540_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_48540'>持钱就人卜，敲瓦隔林鸣。<div id='poem_sentence_9_48540_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_48540'>卜得山上<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作上山）</span>卦，归来桑枣下。<div id='poem_sentence_10_48540_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_48540'>吹火向白茅<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作苇）</span>，腰镰映赪蔗。<div -----title
荆州
-----detail

href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=861&endYear=861')">861年</a>　是年春，自襄阳抵江陵，在荆南节度使萧鄴幕为从事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=861&endYear=861')">861年</a>　在荆南幕期间，有《答段柯古赠葫芦管笔状》<div id='poem_1375702' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1375702' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1375702?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答段柯古赠葫芦管笔状</a><span class='authorDate'>（861年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18032, "唐", "温庭筠", "poem_title_1375702")'>温庭筠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1375702_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1375702'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1375702'>庭筠累日来洛水寒疝。荆州夜嗽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1375702_comment'></div>筋骸莫摄。邪蛊相攻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1375702_comment'></div>蜗睕伤明。对兰缸而不寝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1375702_comment'></div>牛肠治嗽。嗟药录而难求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1375702_comment'></div>前者伏蒙雅赐葫芦笔管一茎。久欲含词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1375702_comment'></div>聊申拜贶。而上池未效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1375702_comment'></div>下笔无聊。惭恍沈吟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1375702_comment'></div>幽怀未叙。然则产于何地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1375702_comment'></div>得自谁人。而能絜以裁筠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1375702_comment'></div>轻同举羽。岂伊蓍草。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1375702_comment'></div>空操九寸之长。何必灵芝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1375702_comment'></div>独号三株之秀。但曾藏戢册省。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1375702_comment'></div>永贮仙居。却笑遗民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1375702_comment'></div>迁兹佳种。惟应仲履。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1375702_comment'></div>忽压烦声。岂常见己堕遗犀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1375702_comment'></div>仍抽直干。青松所筑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1375702_comment'></div>漆竹藏珍。足使玳瑁惭华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1375702_comment'></div>琉璃掩耀。一枚为贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1375702_comment'></div>岂异陆生。三寸见珍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1375702_comment'></div>遂兼扬子。谨当刊于岩竹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1375702_comment'></div>寘以郊翰。随纤管而为床。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1375702_comment'></div>拟凌云而作屋。所恨书裙寡媚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1375702_comment'></div>钉帐无功。实腼凡姿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1375702_comment'></div>空尘异贶。庭筠状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1375702_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1375702_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=861&endYear=861')">861年</a>　在荆南幕期间，有《游南塘寄知者》<div id='poem_48444' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_48444' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/48444?labeling=true' target='_blank'>游南塘寄知者<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作王知白）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（861年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18032, "唐", "温庭筠", "poem_title_48444")'>温庭筠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_48444_comment'></div><div id='poem_sentence_1_48444_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_48444'>楚水晓<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作晚）</span>凉催客早，杜陵秋思傍蝉多。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=861&endYear=861')">861年</a>　春在荆南幕期间，或作有《西江贻钓叟骞生》，姑系于此。<div id='poem_48326' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_48326' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a -----title
洛阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='10f66900fbdf41c4bd3eb4727288af65_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("10f66900fbdf41c4bd3eb4727288af65");'><span id='10f66900fbdf41c4bd3eb4727288af65_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=862&endYear=862')">862年</a>，62岁</div><div id='10f66900fbdf41c4bd3eb4727288af65' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=862&endYear=862')">862年6月</a>　夏末秋初（六月末或七月初）已在长安或洛阳，作《和太常段少卿东都修行里有嘉莲》，此诗或即作于洛阳，姑系于此。<div id='poem_48356' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_48356' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/48356?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和太常杜少卿东都脩行里有嘉莲</a><span class='authorDate'>（862年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18032, "唐", "温庭筠", "poem_title_48356")'>温庭筠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_48356_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_48356'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_48356'>春秋罢注直铜龙，旧宅嘉莲照水红。<div id='poem_sentence_0_48356_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_48356'>两处<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_48356", 48356, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>龟巢</span>清露里，一时鱼跃翠茎东。<div id='poem_sentence_1_48356_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_48356'>同心表瑞荀池上，半面分妆乐镜中。<div id='poem_sentence_2_48356_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_48356'>应为<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_48356", 48356, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>临川</span>多丽句，故持重艳向西风。<div id='poem_sentence_3_48356_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_48356'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_48356_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end
